15/11/2022, 13:03 - Piyush: import java.util.*;
public class generic_programming {
static Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
static void check_palindrome()
{
System.out.println("enter number of elements you want to enter");
int n=sc.nextInt();
System.out.println("enter the list of strings");
ArrayList<String> word= new ArrayList<String>();

for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
{
String newelement=sc.next();
word.add(newelement);
}
int c=0;
for(String w:word)
{
StringBuilder s1=new StringBuilder(w);
if(w.equals(s1.reverse().toString()))
{
System.out.println(w+" is palindrome");
c++;
}
}
System.out.println("number of strings that are palindome : "+c);

}
static void check_odd_even_or_prime() {
System.out.println("-----MENU-----");
System.out.println("1.odd or even");
System.out.println("2.prime or not");
System.out.println("enter your choice");
int choice=sc.nextInt();

if(choice==1)
{
System.out.println("enter number of elements you want to enter");
int n=sc.nextInt();
System.out.println("enter the integer arraylist");
ArrayList<Integer> p =new ArrayList<Integer>();
for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
{
int x=sc.nextInt();
p.add(x);
}
int e=0,o=0;
for(Integer element:p)
{
if(element%2==0)
{
System.out.println("Even number");
e++;
}
else
{
System.out.println("Odd number");
o++;
}
}
System.out.println("Arraylist contains "+e+" even numbers and "+o+" odd numbers");

}
else if(choice==2)
{
System.out.println("enter number of elements you want to enter");
int n=sc.nextInt();
System.out.println("enter the integer arraylist");
ArrayList<Integer> p =new ArrayList<Integer>();
for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
{
int x=sc.nextInt();
p.add(x);
}
int prime=0,np=0;
for(Integer element:p)
{int flag=0;
if(element==1 || element==0)
flag=1;
for(int i=2;i*i<=element;i++)
{
if(element%i==0)
flag=1;

}
if(flag==0)
{
System.out.println(element+" is Prime number");
prime++;
}
else
{
System.out.println(element+" is not a Prime number");
np++;
}
}
System.out.println("Arraylist contains "+prime+" even numbers and "+np+" odd numbers");
}
else
System.out.println("Invalid choice");

}
public static void main(String []args)
{

System.out.println("-----MENU-----");
System.out.println("1.String");
System.out.println("2.Number");
System.out.println("enter your choice");
int ch=sc.nextInt();
if (ch==1)
check_palindrome();
else if(ch==2)
check_odd_even_or_prime();
else
System.out.println("Invalid choice");



}
}

22/11/2022, 21:31 - Pratik Vairat: import java.util.*;
class Generics{
    Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
    List<Integer> num=new ArrayList<Integer>();
    List<String> str=new ArrayList();
    void inputStr(int n){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            String word=sc.nextLine();
            str.add(word);
        }
    }
    void inputNum(int n){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            int element=sc.nextInt();
            num.add(element);
        }
    }
    void checkPrime(){
        for(int integer:num){        
            boolean flag=true;
            for(int i=2;i<integer/2;i++){
		        if(integer%i==0){
		            flag=false;
		        }
		    }
		    if(flag){
		        System.out.println("Number is Prime: "+integer);
		    }else{
		        System.out.println("Number is not prime :"+integer);
		    }
        }
        
    }
    void oddEven(){
        for(int num:num){
            if(num==0 || num==1){
		        System.out.println("Can Not Predict For 0 or 1: "+num);
		    }
		    if(num%2==0){
		        System.out.println("You Entered Even Number : "+num);
		    }
		    if(num%2!=0){
		        System.out.println("You Entered Odd Number  : "+num);
		    }
        }
    }
    void palindrome(){
        for(String st:str){
            boolean flag=true;
            for(int i=0;i<st.length();i++){
		        if(st.charAt(i)!=st.charAt(st.length()-1-i)){
		            flag=false;
		            break;
		        }
		    }
		    if(flag){
		        System.out.println("String is palindrome : "+st);
		    }else{
		        System.out.println("String is not palindrome");
		    }
        }
    }
    
    
}
public class Main{
	public static void main(String[] args) {
	    Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
	    char cr;
	    do{ 
	        Generics generic=new Generics();
	        System.out.println("Choose datatype to perform operation: ");
	        System.out.println("1. Integer \n2. String (To check Palindrome)\n********************");
	        int op=sc.nextInt();
	        switch(op){
	            case 1:
	                System.out.println("Enter size on list: ");
	                int size=sc.nextInt();
	                System.out.println("Enter List of Elements :");
	                generic.inputNum(size);
	                System.out.println("Chose Operation :\n1.Check Prime Numbers \n2. Check Odd Or Even\n********************");
	                int ch=sc.nextInt();
	                if(ch==1){
	                    generic.checkPrime();
	                }else if(ch==2){
	                    generic.oddEven();
	                }else{
	                    System.out.println("Invalid Input");
	                }
	                break;
	           case 2:
	               System.out.println("Enter List size: ");
	               int sizeStr=sc.nextInt();
	               generic.inputStr(sizeStr);
	               generic.palindrome();
	               break;
	           default:
	                System.out.println("Invalid Input");
	                break;
	        }
	        System.out.println("********************\nDo You Want to perform more Operations ?[Y/N]\n********************");
	        cr=sc.next().charAt(0);
	    }while(cr=='y' || cr=='Y');
	}
}

07/12/2022, 11:50 - +91 88305 81591: interface Car
{
    int  speed=60;
    public void distanceTravelled();
}
interface Bus
{
    int distance=100;
    public void speed();
}
public class Vehicle  implements Car,Bus
{
    int distanceTravelled;
    int averageSpeed;
    public void distanceTravelled()
    {
        distanceTravelled=speed*distance; 
        System.out.println("Total Distance Travelled is : "+distanceTravelled);
    }
    public void speed()
    {
        int averageSpeed=distanceTravelled/speed;
        System.out.println("Average Speed maintained is : "+averageSpeed);
    }
    public static void main(String args[])
    {
        Vehicle v1=new Vehicle();
        v1.distanceTravelled();
        v1.speed();
    }
}

09/12/2022, 10:57 - Omkar Mane: // Program for Tree Traversal
#include<iostream>
using namespace std;
#define max 15

class TreeNode
{
public :
char Data;
TreeNode *Lchild;
TreeNode *Rchild;
};
class stack
{
char str[max];
TreeNode *stk[max];
int data, top;
public:
stack()
{
top=-1;
}
int isEmpty()
{
	if(top==-1)
	    return 1;
	else
		return 0;
}
int isFull()
{
	if(top==max-1)
	    return 1;
	else
		return 0;
}

void Push(TreeNode *x)
{
	top++;
	stk[top] =  x;
}
TreeNode *Pop()
{
	TreeNode *x;
	x = stk[top--];
	return x;
}
};

class BinaryTree
{

public :
TreeNode *Root;
BinaryTree ( ) { Root = NULL; } // constructor
TreeNode * GetNode();
void create();
void Postorder ( TreeNode * );
void Inorder (TreeNode * );
void Preorder (TreeNode * );
void Postorder_Non_Recursive (TreeNode *Root);
void Inorder_Non_Recursive ( TreeNode * Root) ;
void Preorder_Non_Recursive ( TreeNode *Root);
};

void BinaryTree::create()
{
 char ans;
 int key;
 TreeNode *curr,*previous,*temp;
 do
 {
	 curr=new TreeNode;

	 cout<<"Enter the data to construct the tree: ";
	 cin>>curr->Data;
	 curr->Lchild=NULL;
	 curr->Rchild=NULL;
	 if(Root==NULL)
		 Root=curr;
	 else
	 {
	   temp=Root;
	   while(1)
	   {
	      cout<<"\nDo u want left or right child for(l/r) "<<temp->Data ;
	      cin>>ans;
		   if(ans=='l')
		   {
			 if(temp->Lchild==NULL)
			 {
				temp->Lchild=curr;
				break;
			 }
			 else
			      temp=temp->Lchild;
		    }
		    else if(ans=='r')
		    {
			  if(temp->Rchild==NULL)
			  {
				temp->Rchild=curr;
				break;
			  }
			  else
				temp=temp->Rchild;
		    }
	   }
	   }
	   cout<<"\n\tDo u want to continue(1/0)";
	   cin>>key;
 }while(key==1);
}


void BinaryTree :: Inorder (TreeNode * Root)
{
if(Root!=NULL)
{
Inorder (Root -> Lchild);
cout <<"\t"<< Root ->Data;
Inorder (Root ->Rchild);
}
}

void BinaryTree :: Preorder (TreeNode * Root)
{
if(Root!=NULL)
{
cout <<"\t"<< Root ->Data;
Preorder (Root -> Lchild);
Preorder (Root ->Rchild);
}
}

void BinaryTree :: Postorder (TreeNode *Root)
{
if (Root!=NULL)
{
Postorder (Root->Lchild);
Postorder (Root-> Rchild);
cout <<"\t"<< Root->Data;
}
}
void BinaryTree :: Preorder_Non_Recursive ( TreeNode *Root)
{
TreeNode *Tmp = Root;
stack S;
int top=-1;
cout<<"Non-Recursive Pre-Order Traversal = ";
while(1)
{
while(Tmp!=NULL)
// traverse left till left is null and push
{
S.Push(Tmp);
cout<<"\t"<< Tmp ->Data;
Tmp=Tmp->Lchild;
}
if ( S.isEmpty()) return;
//if stack is not empty then pop one and go to right
Tmp=S.Pop();
Tmp=Tmp ->Rchild;
// if stack is empty stop the process
}
}
void BinaryTree :: Inorder_Non_Recursive ( TreeNode *Root)
{
int top=-1;
TreeNode *Tmp;
stack S;
Tmp = Root;
cout<<"Non-Recursive In-Order Traversal = ";
while(1)
{
while (Tmp!=NULL)
{
S.Push (Tmp);
Tmp = Tmp->Lchild;
}
if (S.isEmpty ())
return;
//if stack is not empty then pop one and go to right
Tmp =S.Pop();
if(Tmp!=0)
cout<< Tmp ->Data;
else
cout<<"\n\t Empty Stack";
Tmp = Tmp->Rchild;
}
}

void BinaryTree :: Postorder_Non_Recursive (TreeNode *Root)
{
int i=0,top=-1;
TreeNode * Tmp = Root,*stack[max];
char str1[max],str2[max];

char flag;
// stack S stores node and S1 stores flag â€˜Lâ€™ or â€˜Râ€™
cout<<"Non-Recursive Post-Order Traversal = ";
while (top!=-1||Tmp!=NULL)
{
while (Tmp!=NULL)
// traverse tree left till not NULL
{
if(top!=max-1)
{
top++;
stack[top]=Tmp;
str1[i]=Tmp->Data;
str2[i]='L';
i++;
}
Tmp=Tmp->Lchild;
}
if(top!=-1)
{
	while(str2[i-1]=='R')
	{
		i--;
		cout<<str1[i];
	}
	str2[i-1]='R';
	Tmp =stack[top];
	top--;
	Tmp=Tmp->Rchild;
}
}
for(int j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
{
cout<<str1[j]<<"\t";
}
}
int main()
{
	BinaryTree t1;
  int y,z;
  t1.create();
  do
  {       cout<<"\n****** Tree Traversal *************";
	  cout<<"\n\n\t1.recurssive INORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t2.recurssive PREORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t3.recurssive POSTORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t4.non recurssive INORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t5.non recurssive PREORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t6.non recurssive POSTORDER";
	  cout<<"\n\t7.Exit";
	  cout<<"\n Enter your choice";
	  cin>>y;
	  switchğŸ‘
	  {
	     case 1:
			cout<<"\n Recursive In-Order Traversal = ";
			t1.Inorder(t1.Root);
		 break;
	     case 2:
			cout<<"\n Recursive Pre-Order Traversal = ";
			t1.Preorder(t1.Root);
		 break;
		case 3:
			cout<<"\n Recursive Post-Order Traversal = ";
			   t1.Postorder(t1.Root);
	    break;
	case 4:
	t1.Inorder_Non_Recursive(t1.Root);
	 break;
       case 5:
	t1.Preorder_Non_Recursive(t1.Root);
	 break;
       case 6:
      t1.Postorder_Non_Recursive(t1.Root);
	    break;
       case 7:
	exit(0);
	    break;
       }
  }while(y!=7);
  return 0;
}

15/01/2023, 18:00 - Nikitabai Khuspe: Dear Pune University,
I'm *Your name* and studying in *College name* . I am writing to request a postponement of the end-ofsemester exams for second year engineering students.
I understand that exams are an important part of the educational process and serve as a measure of 
student progress. However, I am concerned that there is not enough time between the end of the insemester exams and the start of the end-of-semester exams to adequately prepare.
As you may be aware, the in-semester exams ended on 20 jan 2023and the end-of-semester exams are 
scheduled to begin on 25 jan2023 This leaves only 4 days for students to review material and 
prepare for the exams.
I believe that a shorter preparation time will not allow students to perform to the best of their ability
and may result in lower exam scores. I therefore request that the end-of-semester exams be 
postponed to allow students more time to review and prepare.
I understand that a postponement may cause inconvenience, but I believe that it is in the best 
interest of the students to have adequate time to prepare for these important exams. I am willing to 
work with the university to find a solution that is fair to all parties involved.
I hope that you will consider my request and grant us fot extra time we need to succeed.

Your sincerely,
*Your name*

07/06/2023, 12:57 - Varun : Trinity: #include <GL/glut.h>
#include <iostream>

using namespace std;

int r;

void E_way(int x, int y) {
    glBegin(GL_POINTS);
    glVertex2i(x, y);
    glVertex2i(-x, y);
    glVertex2i(x, -y);
    glVertex2i(-x, -y);
    glVertex2i(y, x);
    glVertex2i(-y, x);
    glVertex2i(y, -x);
    glVertex2i(-y, -x);
    glEnd();
}

void B_circle() {
    float d;
    d = 3 - 2 * r;
    int x = 0;
    int y = r;

    while (x <= y) {
        E_way(x, y);
        if (d < 0) {
            d = d + 4 * x + 6;
        } else {
            d = d + 4 * (x - y) + 10;
            y--;
        }
        x++;
    }

    glFlush();
}

void init() {
    glClearColor(1, 1, 1, 0);
    glColor3f(1, 0, 0);
    gluOrtho2D(-320, 320, -240, 240);
    glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);
}

int main(int argc, char** argv) {
    cout << "\nEnter Radius: ";
    cin >> r;

    glutInit(&argc, argv);
    glutInitDisplayMode(GLUT_SINGLE | GLUT_RGB);
    glutInitWindowPosition(100, 100);
    glutInitWindowSize(640, 480);
    glutCreateWindow("Bresenham Circle");

    init();

    glutDisplayFunc(B_circle);
    glutMainLoop();

    return 0;
}
